['TC_NC_0001', 'WYUtil triangulate_mesh function testing normal case 0001', 'Testing if the mesh object is properly triangulated through "triangulate_mesh" function, which primitive is created with code "bpy.ops.mesh.primitive_cube_add(location=(0,0,0), rotation=(0,0,0))" generates the default Blender cube on location (0,0,0) with rotation (0,0,0) resulting len(cube.data.polygons) == 12 ', 'WYMesh', 'triangulate_mesh', 'void', 'wymesh', 'bpy.ops.mesh.primitive_cube_add(location=(0,0,0), rotation=(0,0,0))', 'len(cube.data.polygons) == 12', 'len(cube.data.polygons) == 6', '(0,0,0)', '(0,0,0)', 'default Blender cube on location (0,0,0) with rotation (0,0,0)', 'TestCube0001', '', '', '        bpy.ops.mesh.primitive_cube_add(location=(0,0,0), rotation=(0,0,0))\n        cube = bpy.context.object\n        cube.name = "TestCube0001"\n        wyutil = WYUtil()\n        self.assertTrue(len(cube.data.polygons) == 6)\n        wyutil.triangulate_mesh(cube.data)\n        self.assertTrue(len(cube.data.polygons) == 12)']
